2025 register
                  
CREATE TABLE register (
    S_ID varchar REFERENCES Student(S_ID) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    Drive_ID varchar REFERENCES Drive(Drive_ID) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    Registration_Date DATE,
    Is_Interested BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    Reason_If_Not_Interested TEXT,
    CONSTRAINT registers_pk PRIMARY KEY (S_ID, Drive_ID)
);

Placement_Coordinators
DDL Statements
CREATE TABLE Placement_Coordinators (
    PC_ID VARCHAR(10) PRIMARY KEY,
 S_ID VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL REFERENCES Student(S_ID) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    Role VARCHAR(50)
);

Company_Assigned


CREATE TABLE Company_Assigned (
    C_ID VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL REFERENCES Company(C_ID) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    PC_ID VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL REFERENCES Placement_Coordinators(PC_ID) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    PRIMARY KEY (C_ID, PC_ID)
);

Selection_Round
CREATE TABLE Selection_Round (
   Round_ID SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
   Job_Role_ID VARCHAR(10) REFERENCES Job_Role(Job_Role_ID) ON DELETE CASCADE,
   Round_Number INT NOT NULL,  -- 1, 2, 3, etc.
   Round_Type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL CHECK (Round_Type IN
       ('Aptitude Test', 'Technical Test',
        'Technical Interview', 'HR Interview', 'Case Study',
        'Coding Test')
   ),
   Duration_Minutes INT,
      Cutoff_Score DECIMAL(5,2),  -- Minimum score to pass
   Is_Completed BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
   UNIQUE (Job_Role_ID, Round_Number)
);


select * from Selection_Round;
delete from Selection_Round;
-- Set seed for reproducibility
SELECT setseed(0.42);
-- Step 1: Randomly select job roles for rounds
WITH job_roles_list AS (
   SELECT Job_Role_ID
   FROM (VALUES
       ('JR_0002'), ('JR_0008'), ('JR_0009'), ('JR_0013'), ('JR_0014'),
       ('JR_0019'), ('JR_0024'), ('JR_0026'), ('JR_0027'), ('JR_0032'),
       ('JR_0034'), ('JR_0035'), ('JR_0038'), ('JR_0039'), ('JR_0044'),
       ('JR_0055'), ('JR_0062'), ('JR_0067'), ('JR_0079'), ('JR_0082'),
       ('JR_0085'), ('JR_0088'), ('JR_0089'), ('JR_0096'), ('JR_0102'),
       ('JR_0103'), ('JR_0117'), ('JR_0123'), ('JR_0125'), ('JR_0132'),
       ('JR_0151'), ('JR_0158'), ('JR_0165'), ('JR_0172'), ('JR_0181'),
       ('JR_0183'), ('JR_0187'), ('JR_0191'), ('JR_0196'), ('JR_0200'),
       ('JR_0208'), ('JR_0209'), ('JR_0210'), ('JR_0223'), ('JR_0224'),
       ('JR_0229'), ('JR_0231'), ('JR_0234'), ('JR_0236'), ('JR_0237'),
       ('JR_0244'), ('JR_0257'), ('JR_0259'), ('JR_0264'), ('JR_0265'),
       ('JR_0266'), ('JR_0271'), ('JR_0272'), ('JR_0292'), ('JR_0298'),
       ('JR_0299'), ('JR_0305'), ('JR_0308'), ('JR_0316'), ('JR_0317'),
       ('JR_0320'), ('JR_0328'), ('JR_0331'), ('JR_0332'), ('JR_0335'),
       ('JR_0336'), ('JR_0339'), ('JR_0347'), ('JR_0352'), ('JR_0354'),
       ('JR_0359'), ('JR_0360'), ('JR_0369'), ('JR_0371'), ('JR_0374'),
       ('JR_0376'), ('JR_0380'), ('JR_0391'), ('JR_0406'), ('JR_0412'),
       ('JR_0421'), ('JR_0437'), ('JR_0439'), ('JR_0446'), ('JR_0447'),
       ('JR_0460'), ('JR_0462'), ('JR_0464'), ('JR_0466'), ('JR_0471'),
       ('JR_0473'), ('JR_0483'), ('JR_0484'), ('JR_0582'), ('JR_0583'),
       ('JR_0591'), ('JR_0610'), ('JR_0617'), ('JR_0633'), ('JR_0635'),
       ('JR_0662'), ('JR_0663'), ('JR_0730'), ('JR_0731'), ('JR_0738'),
       ('JR_0739'), ('JR_0751'), ('JR_0756'), ('JR_0758'), ('JR_0763'),
       ('JR_0766'), ('JR_0767'), ('JR_0769'), ('JR_0776'), ('JR_0777'),
       ('JR_0785'), ('JR_0812'), ('JR_0813'), ('JR_0875'), ('JR_0884'),
       ('JR_0885'), ('JR_0892'), ('JR_0899'), ('JR_0900'), ('JR_0905'),
       ('JR_0911'), ('JR_0915'), ('JR_0916'), ('JR_0924'), ('JR_0925'),
       ('JR_0931'), ('JR_0939'), ('JR_0940'), ('JR_0953'), ('JR_0954'),
       ('JR_0961'), ('JR_0966'), ('JR_0994'), ('JR_1024'), ('JR_1029'),
       ('JR_1031'), ('JR_1035'), ('JR_1037'), ('JR_1048'), ('JR_1055'),
       ('JR_1056'), ('JR_1060'), ('JR_1061'), ('JR_1073'), ('JR_1075'),
       ('JR_1082'), ('JR_1084'), ('JR_1085'), ('JR_1101'), ('JR_1102'),
       ('JR_1103'), ('JR_1109'), ('JR_1128'), ('JR_1129'), ('JR_1136'),
       ('JR_1137'), ('JR_1138'), ('JR_1162'), ('JR_1163'), ('JR_1164'),
       ('JR_1165'), ('JR_1166'), ('JR_1179'), ('JR_1180'), ('JR_1187'),
       ('JR_1188'), ('JR_1189'), ('JR_1190'), ('JR_1192'), ('JR_1193'),
       ('JR_1205'), ('JR_1211'), ('JR_1226'), ('JR_1228'), ('JR_1229'),
       ('JR_1230'), ('JR_1239'), ('JR_1242'), ('JR_1252'), ('JR_1254'),
       ('JR_1282'), ('JR_1283'), ('JR_1284')
   ) AS t(Job_Role_ID)
),
shuffled_roles AS (
   SELECT
       Job_Role_ID,
       ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY random()) AS rn
   FROM job_roles_list
),
categorized_roles AS (
   SELECT
       Job_Role_ID,
       CASE
           WHEN rn <= 30 THEN 2  -- First 30 roles with 2 rounds
           WHEN rn <= 35 THEN 3  -- Next 5 roles with 3 rounds
           ELSE 1  -- Remaining roles with 1 round
       END AS num_rounds
   FROM shuffled_roles
),
-- Define valid round type combinations (each round has unique round number)
round_combinations AS (
   SELECT * FROM (VALUES
       -- Pattern 1: Aptitude (R1) -> Technical Interview (R2) -> HR Interview (R3)
       (1, 1, 'Aptitude Test'),
       (1, 2, 'Technical Interview'),
       (1, 3, 'HR Interview'),
       -- Pattern 2: Coding (R1) -> Group Discussion (R2) -> HR Interview (R3)
       (2, 1, 'Coding Test'),
       (2, 2, 'Group Discussion'),
       (2, 3, 'HR Interview'),
       -- Pattern 3: Technical Test (R1) -> Case Study (R2) -> HR Interview (R3)
       (3, 1, 'Technical Test'),
       (3, 2, 'Case Study'),
       (3, 3, 'HR Interview'),
       -- Pattern 4: Aptitude (R1) -> Case Study (R2) -> HR Interview (R3)
       (4, 1, 'Aptitude Test'),
       (4, 2, 'Case Study'),
       (4, 3, 'HR Interview'),
       -- Pattern 5: Coding (R1) -> Technical Interview (R2) -> HR Interview (R3)
       (5, 1, 'Coding Test'),
       (5, 2, 'Technical Interview'),
       (5, 3, 'HR Interview'),
       -- Pattern 6: Technical Test (R1) -> Group Discussion (R2) -> HR Interview (R3)
       (6, 1, 'Technical Test'),
       (6, 2, 'Group Discussion'),
       (6, 3, 'HR Interview')
   ) AS t(pattern_id, round_number, round_type)
),
job_patterns AS (
   SELECT
       Job_Role_ID,
       num_rounds,
       (ASCII(SUBSTRING(Job_Role_ID FROM 4)) % 6) + 1 AS pattern_id
   FROM categorized_roles
)
-- Generate rounds for each job role based on assigned pattern
INSERT INTO Selection_Round
(Job_Role_ID, Round_Number, Round_Type, Duration_Minutes, Cutoff_Score)
SELECT
   jp.Job_Role_ID,
   rc.round_number,
   rc.round_type,
   CASE (random() * 3)::INT
       WHEN 0 THEN 45
       WHEN 1 THEN 50
       ELSE 60
   END,
   45 + (random() * 55)::INT
FROM job_patterns jp
JOIN round_combinations rc ON jp.pattern_id = rc.pattern_id
WHERE rc.round_number <= jp.num_rounds
ORDER BY jp.Job_Role_ID, rc.round_number;
